The schema is given below:\n    47→ *\n    48→ * RecordBatch =>\n    49→ *  BaseOffset => Int64\n    50→ *  Length => Int32\n    51→ *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n    52→ *  Magic => Int8\n    53→ *  CRC => Uint32\n    54→ *  Attributes => Int16\n    55→ *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n    56→ *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n    57→ *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n    58→ *  ProducerId => Int64\n    59→ *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n    60→ *  BaseSequence => Int32\n    61→ *  RecordsCount => Int32\n    62→ *  Records => [Record]\n    63→ *\n    64→ * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n    65→ * directly following the count of the number of records.\n    66→ *\n    67→ * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\n    68→ * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\n    69→ * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\n    70→ * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\n    71→ * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n    72→ *\n    73→ * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\n    74→ * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\n    75→ * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\n    76→ * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\n    77→ * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\n    78→ * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\n    79→ * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\n    80→ * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\n    81→ *\n    82→ * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\n    83→ * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\n    84→ * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\n    85→ * is expired from lack of activity.\n    86→ *\n    87→ * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\n    88→ * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\n    89→ * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\n    90→ * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\n    91→ *\n    92→ * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\n    93→ * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\n    94→ * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\n    95→ * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n    96→ *\n    97→ * The current attributes are given below:\n    98→ *\n    99→ *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   100→ *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n   101→ *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   102→ */\n   103→public class DefaultRecordBatch extends       final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n   301→        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n   302→        return new RecordIterator() {\n   303→            @Override\n   304→           return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n   314→            }\n   315→            @Override\n   316→            public void close() {}\n   317→        };\n   318→    }\n   319→\n   320→    @Override\n   321→    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n   322→        if (count() == 0)\n   323→            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n   324→\n   325→        if (!isCompressed())\n   326→            return uncompressedIterator();\n   327→\n   328→        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n   329→        // so we decompress The schema is given below:\n *\n * RecordBatch =>\n *  BaseOffset => Int64\n *  Length => Int32\n *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *  Magic => Int8\n *  CRC => Uint32\n *  Attributes => Int16\n *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *  ProducerId => Int64\n *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *  BaseSequence => Int32\n *  RecordsCount => Int32\n *  Records => [Record]\n *\n * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n * directly following the count of the number of records.\n *\n * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\n * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\n * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\n * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\n * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n *\n * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\n * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\n * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\n * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\n * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\n * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\n * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\n * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\n *\n * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\n * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\n * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\n * is expired from lack of activity.\n *\n * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\n * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\n * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\n * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\n *\n * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\n * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\n * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\n * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n *\n * The current attributes are given below:\n *\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET = PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET + PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 2;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + (written < sizeInBytes())\n    88→            written += channel.write(buffer);\n    89→        buffer.reset();\n    90→        return written;\n    91→    }\n    92→\n    93→    /**\n    94→     * This\n    95→     * may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()}.\n    96→     * @return The number of valid bytes\n    97→     */\n    98→    public int validBytes() {\n    99→        if (validBytes >= 0)\n   100→            return validBytes;\n   101→\n   102→        int bytes = 0;\n   103→        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n   104→            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n   105→\n   106→        this.validBytes = bytes;\n   107→        return bytes;\n   108→    }\n   109→\n   110→    @Override\n   111→    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n   112→        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n   113→    }\n   114→\n   115→    /**\n   116→     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\n   117→     * @return first batch size including LOG_OVERHEAD if buffer contains header up to\n   118→     *         magic byte, null otherwise\n   119→     * @throws CorruptRecordException if record size or magic is invalid\n   120→     */\n   121→    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n   122→        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n   123→            return null;\n   124→        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n   125→    }\n   126→\n   127→    /**\n   128→     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n   129→     *\n   130→     * @param filter                      The filter function\n   131→     * @param destinationBuffer           The byte buffer to write the filtered records to\n   132→     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported. For small\n   133→     *                                    record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will\n   134→     *                                    dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\n   135→     *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\n   136→     *                                    performance impact.\n   137→     * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\n   138→     */\n   139→    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n   140→        return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\n   141→    }\n   142→\n   143→    /**\n   144→     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n   145→     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n   146→     */\n   147→    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n   148→                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n   149→        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n   150→        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n   151→        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n   152→            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n   153→            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n   154→            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n   155→\n   156→            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n   157→\n   158→            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n   159→                continue;\n   160→\n   161→            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n   162→                filter);\n   163→            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n   164→            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n   165→            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n   166→            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n   167→\n   168→            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n   169→                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n   170→                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n   171→                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n   172→                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n   173→                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n   174→                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n   175→                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n   176→                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n   177→                } else {\n   178→                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n   179→                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n   180→                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n   181→                    else\n   182→                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n   183→                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n   184→                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n   185→                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n   186→                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n   187→                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n   188→                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n   189→                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n   190→                    }\n   191→                }\n   192→            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n   193→                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n   194→                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n   195→\n   196→                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n   197→                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n   198→                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n   199→                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n   200→                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n   201→                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n   202→            }\n   203→\n   204→            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n   205→            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n   206→            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n   207→            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n   208→                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n   209→                return filterResult;\n   210→            }\n   211→        }\n   212→\n   213→        return filterResult;\n   214→    }\n   215→\n   216→    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n   217→                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n   218→                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n   219→                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n   220→        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n   221→            long maxOffset = -1;\n   222→            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n   223→            // Convert records with old record versions\n   224→            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n   225→            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n   226→            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n   227→                Record record = iterator.next();\n   228→                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n   229→\n   230→                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n   231→                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n   232→                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n   233→\n   234→                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n   235→\n   236→                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n   237→                        containsTombstones = true;\n   238→                    }\n   239→                } else {\n   240→                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n   241→                }\n   242→            }\n   243→            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n   244→        }\n   245→    }\n   246→\n   247→    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n   248→        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n   249→        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n   250→        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n   251→        private final long maxOffset;\n   252→        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n   253→                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n   254→                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n   255→                                  final long maxOffset) {\n   256→            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n   257→            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n   258→            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n   259→            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n   260→        }\n   261→    }\n   262→\n   263→    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n   264→                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n   265→                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n   266→                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n   267→        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n   268→        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n   269→        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n   270→        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n   271→        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n   272→        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n   273→                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n   274→        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n   275→                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n   276→        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n   277→                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n   278→\n   279→        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n   280→        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n   281→                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n   282→                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n   283→                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n   284→\n   285→        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n   286→            builder.append(record);\n   287→\n   288→        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n   289→            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n   290→            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n   291→            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n   292→            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n   293→\n   294→        return builder;\n   295→    }\n   296→\n   297→    /**\n   298→     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n   299→     */\n   300→    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n   301→        return buffer.duplicate();\n   302→    }\n   303→\n   304→    @Override\n   305→    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n   306→        if (position < 0)\n   307→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n   308→        if (position > buffer.limit())\n   309→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n   310→        if (size < 0)\n   311→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n   312→\n   313→        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n   314→        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n   315→        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n   316→        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n   317→        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n   318→        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n   319→        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n   320→        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n   321→        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n   322→        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n   323→        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n   324→        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n   325→\n   326→        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n   327→    }\n   328→\n   329→    @Override\n   330→    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n   331→        return batches;\n   332→    }\n   333→\n   334→    @Override\n   335→    public String toString() {\n   336→        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n   337→                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n   338→                \")\";\n   339→    }\n   340→\n   341→    @Override\n   342→    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n   343→        if (this == o)\n   344→            return true;\n   345→        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n   346→            return false;\n   347→\n   348→        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n   349→\n   350→        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n   351→    }\n   352→\n   353→    @Override\n   354→    public int hashCode() {\n   355→        return buffer.hashCode();\n   356→    }\n   357→\n   358→    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n   359→        public final long currentTime;\n   360→        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n   361→\n   362→        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n   363→            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n   364→            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n   365→        }\n   366→\n   367→        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n   368→            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n   369→            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n   370→            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n   371→                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n   372→                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n   373→                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n   374→            }\n   375→        }\n   376→\n   377→        public enum BatchRetention {\n   378→            DELETE, // Delete the batch without inspecting records\n   379→            RETAIN_EMPTY, // Retain the batch even if it is empty\n   380→            DELETE_EMPTY  // Delete the batch if it is empty\n   381→        }\n   382→\n   383→        /**\n   384→         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n   385→         * check the records individually).\n   386→         */\n   387→        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n   388→\n   389→        /**\n   390→         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log. Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}\n   391→         * is used prior to checking individual record retention. Only records from batches which were not\n   392→         * explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n   393→         */\n   394→        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    public static class FilterResult {\n   398→        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n   399→        private int messagesRead = 0;\n   400→        // Note that `bytesRead` should contain only bytes from batches that have been processed, i.e. bytes from\n   401→        // `messagesRead` and any discarded batches.\n   402→        private int bytesRead = 0;\n   403→        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n   404→        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n   405→        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n   406→        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n   407→        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n   408→\n   409→        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n   410→            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n   411→        }\n   412→\n   413→        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n   414→            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n   415→            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n   416→                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n   417→        }\n   418→\n   419→        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n   420→                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n   421→            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n   422→            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n   423→                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n   424→                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n   425→            }\n   426→            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n   427→            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n   428→            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n   429→        }\n   430→\n   431→        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n   432→            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n   433→                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n   434→            if (maxOffset < 0)\n   435→                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n   436→        }\n   437→\n   438→        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n   439→            return outputBuffer;\n   440→        }\n   441→\n   442→        public int messagesRead() {\n   443→            return messagesRead;\n   444→        }\n   445→\n   446→        public int bytesRead() {\n   447→            return bytesRead;\n   448→        }\n   449→\n   450→        public int messagesRetained() {\n   451→            return messagesRetained;\n   452→        }\n   453→\n   454→        public int bytesRetained() {\n   455→            return bytesRetained;\n   456→        }\n   457→\n   458→        public long maxOffset() {\n   459→            return maxOffset;\n   460→        }\n   461→\n   462→        public long maxTimestamp() {\n   463→            return maxTimestamp;\n   464→        }\n   465→\n   466→        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n   467→            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n   468→        }\n   469→    }\n   470→\n   471→    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n   472→        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n   473→    }\n   474→\n   475→    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n   476→                                               Compression compression,\n   477→ This is used only for reading or\n * modifying in-place an existing buffer of record batches. To create a new buffer see {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder},\n * or one of the {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, byte, Compression, TimestampType, long)} variants.\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    // Construct a writable memory records\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return buffer.limit();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int writeTo(TransferableChannel channel, int position, int length) throws IOException {\n        if (((long) position) + length > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"position+length should not be greater than buffer.limit(), position: \"\n                    + position + \", length: \" + length + \", buffer.limit(): \" + buffer.limit());\n\n        return Utils.tryWriteTo(channel, position, length, buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write all records to the given channel (including partial records).\n     * @param channel The channel to write to\n     * @return The number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any IO errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The total number of bytes in this message set not including any partial, trailing messages. This\n     * may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()}.\n     * @return The number of valid bytes\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\n     * @return first batch size including LOG_OVERHEAD if buffer contains header up to\n     *         magic byte, null otherwise\n     * @throws CorruptRecordException if record size or magic is invalid\n     */\n    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n            return null;\n        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * @param filter                      The filter function\n     * @param destinationBuffer           The byte buffer to write the filtered records to\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported. For small\n     *                                    record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4) will\n     *                                    dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\n     *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\n     *                                    performance impact.\n     * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\n     */\n    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        public final long currentTime;\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            DELETE, // Delete the batch without inspecting records\n            RETAIN_EMPTY, // Retain the batch even if it is empty\n            DELETE_EMPTY  // Delete the batch if it is empty\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log. Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}\n         * is used prior to checking individual record retention. Only records from batches which were not\n         * explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        // Note that `bytesRead` should contain only bytes from batches that have been processed, i.e. bytes from\n        // `messagesRead` and any discarded batches.\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void In older record format versions\n * (magic 0 and 1), a batch contained a single record if uncompressed, but could contain many records\n * with compression. Newer versions (magic 2 and above) typically contain multiple records regardless\n * of compression configuration.\n *\n * <p><strong>Thread Safety:</strong> Implementations of this interface are <em>not thread-safe</em>.\n * External synchronization is required if accessed concurrently.</p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Protocol Role:</strong> RecordBatch is the fundamental serialization unit in Kafka's\n * log segment files. Each batch contains a binary-encoded header with metadata (offsets, timestamps,\n * producer information, attributes), followed by compressed or uncompressed record data. The batch\n * header includes CRC-32C checksum validation to detect corruption.</p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Format Versions:</strong> The interface abstracts over multiple magic versions:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Magic v0: Simple format with checksum, no timestamps or producer info</li>\n *   <li>Magic v1: Adds timestamp support</li>\n *   <li>Magic v2: Introduces producer ID/epoch, sequence numbers, and improved transaction support</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Key Invariants:</strong>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Batch offsets are monotonically increasing across the log</li>\n *   <li>For magic v2+, the base and last offsets from the original batch are preserved through\n *       log compaction to maintain producer state</li>\n *   <li>Checksums cover batch attributes and records (magic byte position varies)</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see CompressionType\n * @see TimestampType\n */\npublic interface RecordBatch extends Iterable<Record> {"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1112,"cache_read_input_tokens":49104,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1112},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e3a0e01f-a865-49a9-ba4f-127bd95afc34","uuid":"38068144-ae9d-47fe-a54a-b9df4da0c88b"}

In old versions of the record format (versions 0 and 1),\n * a batch consisted always of a single record if no compression was enabled, but could contain\n * many records otherwise. Newer versions (magic versions 2 and above) will generally contain many records\n * regardless of compression.\n */\npublic interface RecordBatch extends Iterable<Record> {\n\n    /**\n     * The \"magic\" values\n     */\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V0 = 0;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V1 = 1;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V2 = 2;\n\n    /**\n     * The current \"magic\" value\n     */\n    byte CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE = MAGIC_VALUE_V2;\n\n    /**\n     * Timestamp value for records without a timestamp\n     */\n    long NO_TIMESTAMP = -1L;\n\n    /**\n     * Values used in the v2 record format by non-idempotent/non-transactional producers or when\n     * up-converting from an older format.\n     */\n    long NO_PRODUCER_ID = -1L;\n    short NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH = -1;\n    int NO_SEQUENCE = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Used to indicate an unknown leader epoch, which will be the case when the record set is\n     * first created by the producer.\n     */\n    int NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether the checksum of this batch is correct.\n     *\n     * @return true If so, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Raise an exception if the checksum is not valid.\n     */\n    void ensureValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the checksum of this record batch, which covers the batch header as well as all of the records.\n     *\n     * @return The 4-byte unsigned checksum represented as a long\n     */\n    long checksum();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the max timestamp or log append time of this record batch.\n     *\n     * If the timestamp type is create time, this is the max timestamp among all records contained in this batch and\n     * the value is updated during compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The max timestamp\n     */\n    long maxTimestamp();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the timestamp type of this record batch. This will be {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * if the batch has magic 0.\n     *\n     * @return The timestamp type\n     */\n    TimestampType timestampType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base offset contained in this record batch. For magic version prior to 2, the base offset will\n     * always be the offset of the first message in the batch. This generally requires deep iteration and will\n     * return the offset of the first record in the record batch. For magic version 2 and above, this will return\n     * the first offset of the original record batch (i.e. prior to compaction). For non-compacted topics, the\n     * behavior is equivalent.\n     *\n     * Because this requires deep iteration for older magic versions, this method should be used with\n     * caution. Generally {@link #lastOffset()} is safer since access is efficient for all magic versions.\n     *\n     * @return The base offset of this record batch (which may or may not be the offset of the first record\n     *         as described above).\n     */\n    long baseOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last offset in this record batch (inclusive). Just like {@link #baseOffset()}, the last offset\n     * always reflects the offset of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The offset of the last record in this batch\n     */\n    long lastOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the offset following this record batch (i.e. the last offset contained in this batch plus one).\n     *\n     * @return the next consecutive offset following this batch\n     */\n    long nextOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the record format version of this record batch (i.e its magic value).\n     *\n     * @return the magic byte\n     */\n    byte magic();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer id for this log record batch. For older magic versions, this will return -1.\n     *\n     * @return The producer id or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    long producerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer epoch for this log record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The producer epoch, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    short producerEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Does the batch have a valid producer id set.\n     */\n    boolean hasProducerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #baseOffset()}, this value is not\n     * affected by compaction: it always retains the base sequence number from the original batch.\n     *\n     * @return The first sequence number or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int baseSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #lastOffset()}, the last sequence number\n     * always reflects the sequence number of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The last sequence number or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int lastSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the compression type of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The compression type\n     */\n    CompressionType compressionType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the size in bytes of this batch, including the size of the record and the batch overhead.\n     * @return The size in bytes of this batch\n     */\n    int sizeInBytes();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the count if it is efficiently supported by the record format (which is only the case\n     * for magic 2 and higher).\n     *\n     * @return The number of records in the batch or null for magic versions 0 and 1.\n     */\n    Integer countOrNull();\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this record batch is compressed.\n     * @return true if so, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isCompressed();\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch into a buffer.\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write the batch to\n     */\n    void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer);\n\n    /**\n     * Whether or not this record batch is part of a transaction.\n     * @return true if it is, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isTransactional();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the delete horizon, returns OptionalLong.EMPTY if the first timestamp is not the delete horizon\n     * @return timestamp of the delete horizon\n     */\n    OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the partition leader epoch of this record batch.\n     * @return The leader epoch or -1 if it is unknown\n     */\n    int partitionLeaderEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator which basically delays decompression of the record stream until the records\n     * are actually asked for using {@link Iterator#next()}. If the message format does not support streaming\n     * iteration, then the normal iterator is returned. Either way, callers should ensure that the iterator is closed.\n     *\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported.\n     *                                    For small record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4)\n     *                                    will dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the\n     *                                    batch. As such, a supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant\n     *                                    performance impact.\n     * @return The closeable iterator\n     */\n    CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier);\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this is a control batch (i.e. whether the control bit is set in the batch attributes).\n     * For magic versions prior to 2, this is always false.\n     *\n     * @return Whether this is a batch containing control records\n     */\n    boolean isControlBatch();\n\n    /**\n     * iterate all records to find the offset of max timestamp.\n     * noted:\n     * 1) that the earliest offset will return if there are multi records having same (max) timestamp\n     * 2) it always returns None if the {@link RecordBatch#magic()} is equal to {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V0}\n     * @return offset of max timestamp\n     */\n    default Optional<Long> offsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n        if (magic() == RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V0) return Optional.empty();\n        long maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iter = streamingIterator(BufferSupplier.create())) {\n            while (iter.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iter.next();\n                if (maxTimestamp == record.timestamp()) return Optional.of(record.offset());\n            }\n        }\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n}\n","numLines":270,"startLine":1,"totalLines":270}}}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_011UwoUZ54JM65pSf432UpuT","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_0167XrP1XTauPDmeKT6Z94dA","name":"Bash","input":{"command":"cat > /tmp/RecordBatch.java << 'ENDOFFILE'\n/*\n * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation (ASF) under one or more\n * contributor license agreements. See the NOTICE file distributed with\n * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\n * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\n * (the \"License\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\n * the License. You may obtain a copy of the License at\n *\n *    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n *\n * Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n * distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n * WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n * See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n * limitations under the License.\n */\npackage org.apache.kafka.common.record.internal;\n\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.record.TimestampType;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.BufferSupplier;\nimport org.apache.kafka.common.utils.CloseableIterator;\n\nimport java.nio.ByteBuffer;\nimport java.util.Iterator;\nimport java.util.Optional;\nimport java.util.OptionalLong;\n\n/**\n * A record batch is a container for records in the Kafka protocol. In older record format versions\n * (magic 0 and 1), a batch contained a single record if uncompressed, but could contain many records\n * with compression. Newer versions (magic 2 and above) typically contain multiple records regardless\n * of compression configuration.\n *\n * <p><strong>Thread Safety:</strong> Implementations of this interface are <em>not thread-safe</em>.\n * External synchronization is required if accessed concurrently.</p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Protocol Role:</strong> RecordBatch is the fundamental serialization unit in Kafka's\n * log segment files. Each batch contains a binary-encoded header with metadata (offsets, timestamps,\n * producer information, attributes), followed by compressed or uncompressed record data. The batch\n * header includes CRC-32C checksum validation to detect corruption.</p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Format Versions:</strong> The interface abstracts over multiple magic versions:\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Magic v0: Simple format with checksum, no timestamps or producer info</li>\n *   <li>Magic v1: Adds timestamp support</li>\n *   <li>Magic v2: Introduces producer ID/epoch, sequence numbers, and improved transaction support</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p><strong>Key Invariants:</strong>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>Batch offsets are monotonically increasing across the log</li>\n *   <li>For magic v2+, the base and last offsets from the original batch are preserved through\n *       log compaction to maintain producer state</li>\n *   <li>Checksums cover batch attributes and records (magic byte position varies by version)</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch\n * @see MemoryRecords\n * @see CompressionType\n * @see TimestampType\n */\npublic interface RecordBatch extends Iterable<Record> {\n\n    /**\n     * The \"magic\" values\n     */\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V0 = 0;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V1 = 1;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V2 = 2;\n\n    /**\n     * The current \"magic\" value\n     */\n    byte CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE = MAGIC_VALUE_V2;\n\n    /**\n     * Timestamp value for records without a timestamp\n     */\n    long NO_TIMESTAMP = -1L;\n\n    /**\n     * Values used in the v2 record format by non-idempotent/non-transactional producers or when\n     * up-converting from an older format.\n     */\n    long NO_PRODUCER_ID = -1L;\n    short NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH = -1;\n    int NO_SEQUENCE = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Used to indicate an unknown leader epoch, which will be the case when the record set is\n     * first created by the producer.\n     */\n    int NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether the checksum of this batch is correct.\n     *\n     * @return true if the checksum matches the computed value, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Raise an exception if the checksum is not valid.\n     *\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.CorruptRecordException if the checksum is invalid or the batch size is corrupted\n     */\n    void ensureValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the checksum of this record batch, which covers the batch header as well as all of the records.\n     * The checksum is computed using CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial starting from the attributes field.\n     *\n     * @return the 4-byte unsigned checksum represented as a long\n     */\n    long checksum();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the max timestamp of this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>If the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#CREATE_TIME}, this is the maximum timestamp\n     * among all records contained in this batch. This value may be updated during log compaction.</p>\n     *\n     * <p>If the timestamp type is {@link TimestampType#LOG_APPEND_TIME}, this is the timestamp assigned\n     * by the broker when the batch was appended to the log.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the max timestamp in milliseconds\n     */\n    long maxTimestamp();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the timestamp type of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return the timestamp type, or {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE} if the batch has magic 0\n     */\n    TimestampType timestampType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base offset contained in this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>For magic versions prior to 2, the base offset is always the offset of the first message in the batch.\n     * This generally requires deep iteration through the records.</p>\n     *\n     * <p>For magic version 2 and above, this returns the first offset of the original record batch (i.e. prior to\n     * log compaction). For non-compacted topics, the behavior is equivalent to magic v0-v1.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance Note:</strong> For magic v0-v1, this method requires iterating through all records\n     * and should be used with caution. {@link #lastOffset()} is more efficient across all magic versions.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the base offset of this record batch\n     */\n    long baseOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last offset in this record batch (inclusive).\n     *\n     * <p>Like {@link #baseOffset()}, the last offset always reflects the offset of the last record in the original\n     * batch, even if records are removed during log compaction. This value is efficiently available for all magic versions.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the offset of the last record in this batch\n     */\n    long lastOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the offset following this record batch (i.e. the last offset contained in this batch plus one).\n     *\n     * @return the next consecutive offset following this batch\n     */\n    long nextOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the record format version (magic value) of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return the magic byte: 0, 1, or 2 (or higher for future versions)\n     */\n    byte magic();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer ID for this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>For older magic versions (v0 and v1), this will always return {@link #NO_PRODUCER_ID}.</p>\n     *\n     * <p>For magic v2 and above, returns the producer ID assigned by the broker, or {@link #NO_PRODUCER_ID}\n     * if the batch was produced by a non-idempotent producer.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the producer ID, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    long producerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer epoch for this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>Used in conjunction with {@link #producerId()} to detect duplicate batches in idempotent producers.\n     * The epoch is incremented each time the producer is initialized.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the producer epoch, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    short producerEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this batch has a valid producer ID set.\n     *\n     * @return true if a valid producer ID is present, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean hasProducerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base sequence number of this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>Like {@link #baseOffset()}, this value is not affected by log compaction: it always retains the base\n     * sequence number from the original batch. Used for duplicate detection in idempotent producers.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the first sequence number, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int baseSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last sequence number of this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>Like {@link #lastOffset()}, the last sequence number always reflects the sequence number of the last record\n     * in the original batch, even if records are removed during log compaction.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the last sequence number, or -1 if there is none\n     */\n    int lastSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the compression type applied to records in this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>If compression is enabled, record data following the batch header is compressed using the specified codec,\n     * and the {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} method will decompress on access.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the {@link CompressionType} for this batch\n     */\n    CompressionType compressionType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the size in bytes of this batch, including the batch header overhead and all record data.\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance:</strong> This is an O(1) operation for magic v2+, but may require buffer access\n     * for older formats.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the total size in bytes of this batch\n     */\n    int sizeInBytes();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the count of records in this batch, if efficiently supported by the record format.\n     *\n     * <p>Record count is efficiently available only for magic version 2 and higher. For magic v0 and v1,\n     * this method returns null, requiring iteration to determine the record count.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the number of records in the batch, or null for magic versions 0 and 1\n     */\n    Integer countOrNull();\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this record batch uses compression.\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance Implication:</strong> Compressed batches require decompression before individual\n     * records can be accessed. Consider using {@link #streamingIterator(BufferSupplier)} with a\n     * {@link BufferSupplier} that reuses buffers to minimize allocation overhead.</p>\n     *\n     * @return true if compression is enabled, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isCompressed();\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch into the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance:</strong> This operation performs a shallow copy of the underlying buffer and is O(1).\n     * The buffer position is updated to reflect the bytes written.</p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer the ByteBuffer to write the batch to; must have sufficient remaining capacity\n     */\n    void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer);\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this record batch is part of a transaction.\n     *\n     * <p>Transactional batches contain records from a single producer transaction and may be followed by\n     * commit/abort control markers.</p>\n     *\n     * @return true if this batch is transactional, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isTransactional();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the delete horizon timestamp for this batch, if set.\n     *\n     * <p>The delete horizon is used in log compaction to mark tombstones and transaction markers\n     * for deletion after the specified time. This is set when log cleanup removes records from a batch\n     * containing tombstones or aborted transaction markers.</p>\n     *\n     * @return an {@link OptionalLong} containing the delete horizon timestamp, or empty if not set\n     */\n    OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the partition leader epoch of this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>The leader epoch is used to disambiguate leader changes and prevent inconsistencies during\n     * leader failures. The epoch is assigned by the broker when the batch is written.</p>\n     *\n     * @return the leader epoch, or -1 if it is unknown (typically for batches created by producers)\n     */\n    int partitionLeaderEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator that delays decompression of the record stream until records are actually\n     * accessed via {@link Iterator#next()}.\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance Characteristics:</strong>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>For uncompressed batches, returns a lazy iterator that reads records directly from the buffer</li>\n     *   <li>For compressed batches, wraps the compression codec's input stream and decompresses on demand</li>\n     *   <li>Reusing buffers via the supplied {@link BufferSupplier} significantly improves performance\n     *       for small batches, as allocation overhead can dominate decompression cost (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4)</li>\n     *   <li>The iterator must be closed to free decompression resources</li>\n     * </ul>\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Thread Safety:</strong> The returned iterator is not thread-safe and must not be shared\n     * across threads.</p>\n     *\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier the supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression; reusing buffers\n     *                                    yields significant performance benefits for small batches\n     * @return a {@link CloseableIterator} over the records in this batch; must be closed by the caller\n     */\n    CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier);\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this is a control batch.\n     *\n     * <p>Control batches contain only control messages (e.g., transaction commit/abort markers, leader changes)\n     * and are not intended for user consumption. For magic versions prior to 2, this is always false.</p>\n     *\n     * @return true if this batch contains control records, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isControlBatch();\n\n    /**\n     * Iterate all records in this batch to find the offset of the maximum timestamp.\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Performance:</strong> This method requires iterating through all records in the batch.\n     * For large batches, this can be expensive.</p>\n     *\n     * <p><strong>Behavior Notes:</strong>\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>If multiple records share the same maximum timestamp, the earliest offset is returned</li>\n     *   <li>Always returns empty for batches with magic version 0 (which have no timestamp)</li>\n     * </ul>\n     *\n     * @return an {@link Optional} containing the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp,\n     *         or empty if the batch has no records or magic version 0\n     */\n    default Optional<Long> offsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n        if (magic() == RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V0) return Optional.empty();\n        long maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iter = streamingIterator(BufferSupplier.create())) {\n            while (iter.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iter.next();\n                if (maxTimestamp == record.timestamp()) return Optional.of(record.offset());\n            }\n        }\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n}\nENDOFFILE\necho \"Created RecordBatch.java in /tmp\"\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":159,"cache_read_input_tokens":55726,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":159},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e3a0e01f-a865-49a9-ba4f-127bd95afc34","uuid":"45f42903-e64d-4351-afaf-a3e1379a60c3"}
